scope enforcement through a layered architecture spanning multiple services. The authentication flow begins in the HTTP middleware stack where ContextHandler (pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go) acts as the entry point, calling the Authenticator service to process incoming requests. The ContextHandler.Middleware initializes a ReqContext and invokes authn.Service.Authenticate with an authn.Request containing the HTTP request details.\\n\\nThe authentication service (pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/service.go) orchestrates multiple authentication clients in priority order, including the APIKey client. When the APIKey client (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go) detects an API key in the Authorization header (either as Bearer token or Basic auth with 'api_key' username), it attempts authentication. The client retrieves the API key from the database using either the modern service account token format handled by satokengen (pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go) or the legacy format handled by apikeygen (pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go).\\n\\nAPI key validation occurs in the validateApiKey function (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go), which enforces three critical security checks: expiration validation (comparing key.Expires timestamp against current time), revocation status checking (key.IsRevoked flag), and organization scope enforcement (verifying key.OrgID matches the requested organization). Additionally, the client enforces that API keys must be associated with a service account (key.ServiceAccountId must be non-null).\\n\\nThe API key model (pkg/services/apikey/model.go) contains fields for: Expires (optional timestamp for expiration), IsRevoked (optional boolean flag), ServiceAccountId (links to service account), and Role (organization role type). The APIKey service implementation (pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go) provides the Service interface that includes GetAPIKeyByHash, GetApiKeyByName, AddAPIKey, and UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate methods. The underlying SQL store (pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go) implements database operations including quota scoping with OrgScope and GlobalScope parameters.\\n\\nScope enforcement extends beyond the API key itself through the Identity system. The validateApiKey function checks organization membership, and the resulting Identity object created by newServiceAccountIdentity function contains OrgID for scope isolation. The service account's DefaultOrgRole (set from key.Role in pkg/services/serviceaccounts/database/store.go) determines permission scope. The Identity struct (pkg/services/authn/identity.go) maintains OrgRoles mapping organization IDs to role types, enabling fine-grained access control evaluation through the AccessControl service (pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go).\\n\\nPost-authentication, the Hook method (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go) asynchronously updates the LastUsedAt timestamp in the api_key table, providing audit capabilities for API key usage tracking. The complete authentication chain flows from HTTP middleware through the authenticator service, API key client, database retrieval, validation checks, scope enforcement, and finally identity creation for downstream authorization decisions.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1430,"cache_read_input_tokens":88303,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1430},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0f01fb54-8f67-4169-908d-8ebf01167d43","uuid":"5ab30c3e-b1f3-4415-9a4d-21587550328a"}
